      function livechat(e){
						img=window.open("//helion.pl/livechat.html","Livechat","status=no,toolbar=no,scrollbars=yes,width=980,height=650");
						e.preventDefault();
					    }
					    $(document).ready(function(){
						$.get('https://helion.pl/json/polki.php',{"co":"get"},function(data){
						    var obj = $.parseJSON(data);
						    var ilosc = 0;
						    if(obj.status == 'OK'){
							$('ul.userMenuMobilePolki').html('');
							$.each(obj.lista,function(i,val){
							    $('ul.userMenuMobilePolki').append('<li><a href="/users/konto/polka/'+val.id+'">'+val.nazwa+'</a></li>');
							    ilosc = ilosc + 1;
							});
						    }
						});
					    });

          <script>
           $('#niematakiegoID,#programowanie,#webmasterstwo,#podreczniki-szkolne,#aplikacje-biurowe,#bazy-danych,#big-data,#biznes-it,#cad-cam,#digital-lifestyle,#dtp,#elektronika,#fotografia-cyfrowa,#grafika-komputerowa,#gry,#hacking,#hardware,#matematyka,#pakiety-naukowe,#podstawy-komputera,#programowanie-mobilne,#serwery-internetowe,#sieci-komputerowe,#start-up,#systemy-operacyjne,#technologia-dla-dzieci,#uczenie-maszynowe,#zamowienia-dotacyjne-men,#zestawy').bind( "click", function() {
	    showSubcategories(this);
});
function showSubcategories(id){
    var elems = document.getElementsByClassName(id.id);
    id.innerHTML = "-";
    $(id).bind( "click", function() {
        closeSubcategories(this);
      });
    for(var i = 0; i < elems.length; i++){
	{elems[i].style.display = 'block';}
    }
    $(id).parent().siblings(".kategorieGlowne").css("display", "none");
}
function closeSubcategories(id){
    var elems = document.getElementsByClassName(id.id);
    id.innerHTML = "+";
    $(id).bind( "click", function() {
        showSubcategories(this);
      });
    for(var i = 0; i < elems.length; i++){
	{elems[i].style.display = 'none';}
    }
    $(id).parent().siblings(".kategorieGlowne").css("display", "block");
}
          </script>

    .book-list-container .list .slick-list .slick-track > li:hover .author { visibility: hidden; }
    .book-list-container .list .slick-list .slick-track > li:hover .book-type { position: relative; top: 98px; }
    .book-list-container .list .slick-list .slick-track .short-desc { z-index: 2; position: absolute; display: none; left: -1px; top: 0; color: white; padding: 20px 20px 30px 20px; font-size: 15px; line-height: 25px;}
}

     function calculateHMSleft()
					{
					//calculate
					    var now = new Date();
					    var hoursleft = 23-now.getHours();
					    var minutesleft = 59-now.getMinutes();
					    var secondsleft = 59-now.getSeconds();
					    
					//format 0 prefixes
					    if(minutesleft<10) minutesleft = "0"+minutesleft;
					    if(secondsleft<10) secondsleft = "0"+secondsleft;
					
					//display
					    $('#timer').html("Pozostało "+hoursleft+":"+minutesleft+":"+secondsleft);
					}
					
					calculateHMSleft();
					setInterval(calculateHMSleft, 1000);
$("#przedsprzedaz").click(function(ev) {
    ev.preventDefault();
    $('#przedsprzedaz').parent('li').addClass('active');
    $('#nowosci').parent('li').removeClass('active');
    $('#bookListContainer1').css({display: 'none'});
    $('#bookListContainer2').css({display: 'block'});
    $('#showAll1').html('wszystkie książki w przedsprzedaży');
    $("#showAll1").attr("href", "//helion.pl/kategorie/w-przedsprzedazy");
    $('#bookListContainer2 .slider').slick('setPosition');
});

function odliczam_sw(dzien,miesiac,rok){
    var dzis=new Date();
    var dzis_dzien = dzis.getDate();
    var dzis_miesiac = dzis.getMonth()+1;
    var dzis_rok = dzis.getFullYear();
    if(dzis_rok == rok){
	if(dzis_miesiac == miesiac){
	    if(dzis_dzien <= dzien){
		var ile = dzien - dzis_dzien;
		var text;
		if(ile > 1){ text = " dni"; }
		if(ile == 1){ text = " dzień"; }
		$('#hf2').html(ile + text);
	    }
	}
    }
}
//odliczam_sw(20,12,2017);
var end = new Date('12/21/2016 2:0 PM');
var _second = 1000;
var _minute = _second * 60;
var _hour = _minute * 60;
var _day = _hour * 24;
var timer2;
function showRemaining() {
        var now = new Date();
        var distance = end - now;
        if (distance < 0) {
            clearInterval(timer);
            document.getElementById('countdown').innerHTML = 'EXPIRED!';
            return;
        }
        var days = Math.floor(distance / _day);
        var hours = Math.floor((distance % _day) / _hour);
        var minutes = Math.floor((distance % _hour) / _minute);
        var seconds = Math.floor((distance % _minute) / _second);
        document.getElementById('hf2').innerHTML = hours + ' godzina ';
}

  <script>
   $( document ).ready(function() {
                function getCookie(cname) {
                    var name = cname + "=";
                    var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
                    var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
                    for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
                        var c = ca[i];
                        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                            c = c.substring(1);
                        }
                        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                            return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                        }
                    }
                    return "";
                }
                if(getCookie("helionrodoaccepted") == ""){
                        $(".rodo-accept").show();
                }
		function acceptrodo(){
                	var cookieName = "helionrodoaccepted";
        	        var myDate = new Date();
	                myDate.setMonth(myDate.getMonth() + 12);
                	document.cookie = cookieName +"=" + "accepted" + ";expires=" + myDate   + ";domain=.helion.pl;path=/";
	        }
		$("#rodo-ok").click(function(){
			acceptrodo();
			$(".rodo-accept").hide();
		});
        });
  </script>
